==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null) {
            ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = block.getFirstChildOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
            if (constructorCall != null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall != null) {
            Node parentNode = constructorCall.jjtGetParent();
            if (parentNode instanceof ASTThrowStatement) {
                // Skip if the new object is within a throw statement
                return super.visit(node, data);
            }
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall != null && !(constructorCall.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTThrowStatement)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null && 
```
            node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTForStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTWhileStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoop(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoop(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoop(node, data);
    }

    private Object checkLoop(Node node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) && 
            !node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return data;
    }
}

```
// False negative with break in other for-loop
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.SortedSet;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public class Message {
    private List<Function<Message, Boolean>> filters;

    public Message(Message message) {}

    private SortedSet<Message> getFilteredMessages(List<Message> messages) {
        final SortedSet<Message> result = new TreeSet<>(messages);
        for (Message element : messages) {
            Message event = new Message(element);
            for (Function<Message, Boolean> filter : filters) {
                if (!filter.apply(event)) {
                    result.remove(element);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return result;
    }
}
```

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isViolation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isViolation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isViolation(Object node) {
        if (node instanceof ASTConstructorCall && 
            node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null && 
            node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null) {
            return true;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (isViolation(node.jjtGetChild(i))) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTForStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (containsObjectInstantiation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (containsObjectInstantiation(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean containsObjectInstantiation(Object node) {
        if (node instanceof ASTConstructorCall
                && ((ASTConstructorCall) node).getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && ((ASTConstructorCall) node).getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null) {
            return true;
        }
        
        for (int i = 0; i < ((net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node).jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (containsObjectInstantiation(((net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node).jjtGetChild(i))) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        
        return false;
    }
}

```
// False negative with break in other for-loop
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.SortedSet;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public class Message {
    private List<Function<Message, Boolean>> filters;

    public Message(Message message) {}

    private SortedSet<Message> getFilteredMessages(List<Message> messages) {
        final SortedSet<Message> result = new TreeSet<>(messages);
        for (Message element : messages) {
            Message event = new Message(element);
            for (Function<Message, Boolean> filter : filters) {
                if (!filter.apply(event)) {
                    result.remove(element);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return result;
    }
```

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (hasViolation(node) && !hasException(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (hasViolation(node) && !hasException(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean hasViolation(Node node) {
        return node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class).stream().anyMatch(n -> n.getNthParent(2).equals(node));
    }

    private boolean hasException(Node node) {
        return node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class).isEmpty() && node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class).isEmpty();
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import java.util.List;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTForStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkNode(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkNode(node, data);
    }

    private Object checkNode(Node node, Object data) {
        List<ASTAllocationExpression> allocations = node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTAllocationExpression.class);

        for (ASTAllocationExpression allocation : allocations) {
            if (!isInThrowStatement(allocation) && !isInReturnStatement(allocation)) {
                addViolation(data, allocation);
            }
        }
        return data;
    }

    private boolean isInThrowStatement(ASTAllocationExpression allocation) {
        return allocation.getFirstParentOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) != null;
    }

    private boolean isInReturnStatement(ASTAllocationExpression allocation) {
        return allocation.getFirstParentOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) != null;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
```
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null;
    }

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class) == null
                && !(node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTStatementExpressionList.class) != null 
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }

        if (constructorCall.jjtGetParent().jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTCatchClause) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
```
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: New objects can not be created within loops;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
```

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName()) && methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            if (methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            Node parent = methodCall.jjtGetParent();
            while (!(parent instanceof ASTMethodDeclaration || parent instanceof ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration)) {
                parent = parent.jjtGetParent();
            }
            if (parent instanceof ASTMethodDeclaration) {
                ASTMethodDeclaration methodDeclaration = (ASTMethodDeclaration) parent;
                for (ASTFormalParameter formalParameter : methodDeclaration.findDescendantsOfType(ASTFormalParameter.class)) {
                    if (formalParameter.getType() != null && Collection.class.isAssignableFrom(formalParameter.getType())) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
```
}

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
            if (arrayAllocation == null) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoopBody(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoopBody(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoopBody(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        return checkLoopBody(node, data);
    }

    private Object checkLoopBody(ASTStatement node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTBlock) {
                if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed((ASTBlock) node.jjtGetChild(i))) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTBlock node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if(constructorCall != null && constructorCall.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTForeachStatement) {
            return false;
        }
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);

        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
```

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node.getStatement())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassedInsideLoop(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassedInsideLoop(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassedInsideLoop(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassedInsideLoop(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassedInsideLoop(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null) {
            ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
            ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
            if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
                return false;
            }

            ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
                return false;
            }

            ASTMethodCall methodCall = block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                return false;
            }

            ASTTryStatement tryStatement = block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
            if (tryStatement != null) {
                for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                    if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            }

            return block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                    && block.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression iterable = node.getIterable();
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node.getStatement()) && iterable.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) == null) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(Node node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        if (constructorCall == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);

        if (node instanceof ASTForeachStatement && arrayAllocation != null) {
            for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
                if (node.jjtGetChild(i) == arrayAllocation) {
                    arrayAllocation = null;
                    break;
                }
            }
        }

        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node) && !isForeachOverNewArray(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }

    private boolean isForeachOverNewArray(ASTForeachStatement node) {
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        return arrayAllocation != null && arrayAllocation.jjtGetParent().jjtGetParent() == node;
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
```
