import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        if(arrayAllocation != null && arrayAllocation.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTForeachStatement){
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLocalVariableDeclaration.class) != null && isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTReturnStatement returnStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class);
        if (returnStatement != null && returnStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null;
    }

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
```

public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {

            addViolation(data, node);

        return super.visit(node, data);

        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {

    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {

            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);

        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {

            return false;
        }
        
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }
        
        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        ASTReturnStatement returnStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class);
        ASTThrowStatement throwStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class);

        return (returnStatement == null || returnStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) == null)
                && (throwStatement == null || throwStatement.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) == null);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTReturnStatement returnStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class);
        if (returnStatement != null && returnStatement.jjtGetParent().equals(node)) {
            return true;
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null && breakStatement.jjtGetParent().equals(node)) {
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    }
}

```
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }
```

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null) {
            if ("add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName()) || "toArray".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);

        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        if (arrayAllocation != null && arrayAllocation.jjtGetParent().jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTArgumentList) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {

        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {

        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);

        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null) {
            if ("add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                return false;
            }
            // Added condition to check for 'toArray' method
            if ("toArray".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && "add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);
        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null) {
            if("add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                return false;
            } else if("toArray".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                ASTArgumentList argumentList = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
                if (argumentList != null && argumentList.size() == 1 && argumentList.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTArrayAllocation) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {

        }

    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

    public void checkArray() {
        Car[] cars = new Car[3];
        for(int i = 0; i < cars.length; ++i) {
           cars[i] = new Car();
        }
    }
    public void checkCollection() {
        Collection<Car> cars = new ArrayList<>();
        for(int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {
           cars.add(new Car());
        }
    }

    private static class Car {}
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public AvoidInstantiatingObjectsInLoopsRule() {
        super(ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        if (isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNewObjectAssignedOrPassed(ASTStatement node) {
        ASTConstructorCall constructorCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class);
        ASTArrayAllocation arrayAllocation = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAllocation.class);

        if (constructorCall == null && arrayAllocation == null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTAssignmentExpression assignmentExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        if (assignmentExpression != null && assignmentExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class) != null) {
            return false;
        }

        ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null) {
            if ("add".equals(methodCall.getMethodName()) || "toArray".equals(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        ASTTryStatement tryStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTTryStatement.class);
        if (tryStatement != null) {
            for (ASTCatchClause catchClause : tryStatement.findDescendantsOfType(ASTCatchClause.class)) {
                if (catchClause.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        }

        ASTBreakStatement breakStatement = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBreakStatement.class);
        if (breakStatement != null) {
            return false;
        }

        return node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTThrowStatement.class) == null
                && node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTReturnStatement.class) == null;
    }
}
